I run a business in the Littlerock, CA area and ever since Waste Management took over for Benz, there has been nothing but problems. Like another customer review said this last Thanksgiving week they never showed up at all. As I traveled in Mandarin speaking locations in Asia, Taiwan, Shanghai for business purposes, I decided to learn the language. I have been attending Mandarin classes mainly in Winter for about 5 years. First to learn, then to  keep what I learned current when not traveling.

Since 2016 I have been trying to learn Mandarin. I started with Duolingo, and while the app isn't terrible, it was no way for me to learn Mandarin successfully. By the time I had gotten to the end of 2018 all I knew how to say was "hello" and "thank you".

On a whim I decided to look for language classes in the Bay Area and I signed up for the San Jose Learning Center. It was an amazing decision! The classes are very clearly well thought out. If you are considering learning a new language, I would highly recommend signing up for the San Jose Learning Center. It is definitely worth the time and money!!<//text>

<time>1554415220579<//time><text>I have been learning Mandarin from Larry from level 2 to level 6 through classes offered at work. When I switched jobs a year ago, I found out that Larry is teaching the same level Mandarin class at my new workplace, so I was able to continue, and I'm glad I have stuck with it. He is without question the best language teacher I've ever had, for any language.

I have previously taken Mandarin classes at UCSD, and those classes used an older text and emphasized perfect tone pronunciation from the beginning, and it made things very difficult. <text>I have taken Arabic 1 at this location and it has been a great experience. The site has free Wifi, snacks, coffee and tea so if you want to review prior to your session you can sit in the lounge/kitchen area. The class size is small, which is my ideal learning scenario.

Regarding Arabic, the focus in learning is extremely basic (which is much appreciated for a complete beginner). In Arabic 1, you'll learn the Arabic alphabet along with pronunciations, simple word construction, cultural topics and basic vocabulary and greetings.

If you do take a course at this center, discuss the reason why you are learning the language with your instructor and which specific region interests you. This is important since in some languages, there is a pronunciation difference based on region.

My only issue about this location is that the parking lot exit is very low so you need to exit very slowly or else your car's "undercarriage"(?) will scrape the street. Other than this minor issue, I've had a great time learning at this center! shukraan! :)<//text><resp>None<//resp>< Date>

< Text>
I recently completed Korean Level I and Level II classes at San Jose Learning Center. I was interested in learning Korean so that I could better communicate with my Korean in-laws. I was initially really nervous and intimidated to learn a new language, but my Korean instructor Nanmo has been great! She broke down the alphabet and the basic structure of the language - which definitely made it a lot less intimidating. The classes are well paced and definitely doable for someone working full time. It has been rewarding to make progress and to be able to read and write basic Korean. The class sizes at SJLC are generally small and everyone gets sufficient individual attention. Both my classes had ~ 5 students. If you have to miss a class then you can do a brief make-up section for a discounted rate (super good deal!).

The other thing I love about SJLC is the welcoming environment. All the instructors and staff are very friendly. They have water, coffee (definitely necessary after a long work day), and snacks for all the students. They even plan group meet-ups and trips all over the world! It's been a pleasure to get know my classmate as well - we are able to encourage each other along the way and hold each other accountable for making it to class. Many of us will be moving on to Korean 3 and planning some future Korean events as a class.

SJLC also has coupons for returning students and if you make referrals. Overall, these small group classes are a great deal for the price and I would highly recommend for anyone trying to learn a new language!

Lizzie B< /username>
<date>1477520482912< /date>< review>
My family had taken our dog here for years and thought they were okay but never extraordinary. When it was time for our dog to be put down due to old age we chose this place as they had worked with our dog for years. My brother went in to do it because he was the only one who could handle seeing our little guy be put to sleep. When he went in they told that in order to go into the room it was going to be an extra $30 on top of the fee they were charging for the euthanasia. My mom had given him cash to pay and he didn't have extra cash so he left our dog to be put to sleep by himself. It was my brother's judgement call to do that but we think it was really ridiculous to charge to be in the room with your pet, who to many are like family, when he gets put to sleep. The thought that my family dog had to die alone in a room scared and alone will never leave me and I hate this place for putting my brother in the position where he had to make that choice without prior knowledge.< /review>

<Review>One of the worst pet shops I have ever been to. Dozens of animals stuffed into disgustingly tiny tanks. No heaters or enrichment for any of the tropical birds. No air pumps, sumps, or any equipment for the fish tanks (which were all completely FULL of gigantic goldfish). The tanks were egredgiously overstocked and underfiltered. The reptiles had no heat source, many had no hides and were being cohabbed, which is a major NO for animals like leopard geckos, ball pythons, and others that were crammed together when I visited. There were around 10 red slider turtles left in a 3 foot long tank with less than an inch of water in it. There was only one dry area for them, all of the turtles were struggling to sit on the one dry rock under the (I'm hoping it was a heat lamp) heat lamp. No source of temperature control or filter in their tank either. The finches all had overgrown toenails and could hardly move in their cages. Around 6 rats were in each of the 3 tanks for them -these tanks couldn't have been more than 10 gallons each. ALL of the rats had scabs and bloody patches from fighting with one another. The "baby rats" cage (as it was labelled) was completely covered in newspaper, and one of the owners yelled at me when I tried to look inside.

There's signs saying "No pictures!!! No videos!!!" in every corner of the store. If the owners were really taking good care of the animals they have in stock, they wouldn't feel the need to hide what's inside their store. Not to mention, many of the animals have questionable origins. Some of the birds for sale are listed as illegal to own in the state of California, I'm doubtful as to if the owners know this. I'd say it's safe to assume so, unless they're so ashamed of their husbandry that they have to put signs up everywhere saying not to share pictures of their store.

I spent some time talking to and petting their Amazonian blue faced parrot through the cage she was in. When the lady (one of the owners) saw this, she ran over and yelled at me, claiming this bird bites. I'm not trying to call into question the treatment of these animals, but I've worked with very agressive birds before, and this animal nuzzled his face into my hand upon meeting me for the very first time. I really don't see a bird this friendly biting anyone without provocation.

After she yelled at me to stop, the lady ran around the corner of one of the aisles in the store and said something to her husband, who then came around the corner and followed me the rest of the time I was inside. Which wasn't very long, because as soon as I started to look through the goldfish tanks, he told me that the store was closing and that I needed to leave immediately. I asked why, since it was a few hours earlier than the listed closing time on their door. He just said, "No, you need to get out now."

I went across the street (where my bus stop was) and watched as they proceeded to... Not close the store. And let other customers in. For the full 30+ minutes I waited for the bus. Funny how they were so eager to close when I was looking around, but didn't seem to be in a rush once I was gone.

Needless to say, I will not be going back to their location for business. I will do my best to document what I saw and add the photos to my review.

If you've read this far and are looking for a good place to get fish, birds, and other animals, I would HIGHLY RECOMMEND Age of Aquariums in Long Beach, Reptile Factory in Long Beach and Garden Grove, Hong Kong Tropical Fish in Norwalk, Atlantic Tropical Fish in Norwalk (which sells various fish, birds, and some reptiles), and ESPECIALLY Tiki's Tropical Fish in Bellflower (which sells nearly every animal and all you'd need to care for them). These shops have exemplary quality animal care and stocking, and the owners are knowledgeable when it comes to the animals they sell and how to care for them. Please consider doing a little extra driving to support one of these businesses, they really do care about their line of work. I went into the Ramirez pet shop expecting the same, and left dismayed.< /Review><Time>1527917810181</Time><pics>None<//pics><Rating>1</Rating></record>

<user_name>Edwin Posadas< /user_name>< review>
Surprised by most of the posts.  The customer service for me was very good.  The pharmacy was able to utilize my MedImpact coverage which gave several other pharmacies problems.  Also, the use of text alerts and (at times) the CVS app for pickup makes the process much faster.  I have never dropped off a written prescription as all of mine have been e-scripted, but this is the new standard.  Unlike other places, parking is simple and easy and the store is navigable (like most CVS branches) very easily.

I would recommend this CVS to someone who wanted to have an easy pickup with an e-prescription who lives in West LA/Beverly Hills.< /review>
